## 🔑 PAT Capability Report

This spec's Personal Access Token was tested against every relevant Figma REST endpoint. Results:

| Capability | Status | What it unlocks |
|------------|--------|------------------|
| Design Variables | ❌ unavailable | Requires a Figma plan with Variables support (Professional+) and `file_variables:read` scope |
| Named Styles | ❌ unavailable | Text/color/effect styles published to the file |
| Comments | ✅ available | Designer annotations pinned to canvas — needs file view access |
| Dev Resources | ❌ unavailable | Dev Mode attached links (Storybook, tickets, docs) |
| Image Fills | ✅ available | Original source URLs behind raster IMAGE fills |
| Published Components | ✅ available | Author-written descriptions for components/component sets |
| Asset Export URLs | ❌ unavailable | Real downloadable SVG/PNG URLs for extracted icons, illustrations & images |

> ⚠️ **4 capability(ies) unavailable.** This is usually because the file is on a Figma plan that doesn't include that API (e.g. Variables requires Professional+), the token's scope doesn't cover it, or the token owner lacks edit/view access to that data. The rest of this spec was generated using everything that _was_ available.

### Asset Export Instructions

**Icon Library (SVG):** Small, scalable icons for buttons, navigation, and UI elements.

**Illustrations (PNG/SVG):** Larger detailed graphics, patterns, and decorative elements.

**Images (PNG/JPEG):** Raster photographs and complex imagery (property photos, hero images, etc.).

**7442 icons** should be exported as **SVG** for crisp rendering at any scale.

**368 images** should be exported as **PNG** or **JPEG** optimized for web (80-90% quality).

## 📁 Asset Export Checklist

Use the Figma REST API to export assets before building:

### Screen Thumbnails (PNG @2x)
```bash
# Export all screen thumbnails
GET https://api.figma.com/v1/images/MnELadWIBWjZj7w3Yp39KQ?ids=46:304,89:3785,87:1301,87:1300,87:1274,75:564,87:1249,87:1275,75:599,75:679&format=png&scale=2
```

### Vector Icons (SVG)
Extract icons in SVG format for crisp scaling and small file sizes:

```bash
GET https://api.figma.com/v1/images/MnELadWIBWjZj7w3Yp39KQ?ids={ICON_NODE_IDS}&format=svg&scale=2
```

### Raster Images (PNG)
For photographs and complex illustrations:

```bash
GET https://api.figma.com/v1/images/MnELadWIBWjZj7w3Yp39KQ?ids={IMAGE_NODE_IDS}&format=png&scale=2
```

### Using cURL to Download
```bash
curl -X GET "https://api.figma.com/v1/images/MnELadWIBWjZj7w3Yp39KQ?ids=NODE_ID&format=svg" \
  -H "X-Figma-Token: YOUR_TOKEN" \
  -o asset.svg
```

## 🏗️ AI Build Instructions

Use this specification to build the full application. Follow these rules:

### Tech Stack Recommendations
- **Framework:** React (with TypeScript preferred) or Next.js for multi-page apps
- **Styling:** Tailwind CSS — map the colour palette above to a custom `tailwind.config`
- **Icons:** Lucide React or Heroicons (match icon style from designs)
- **Animations:** Framer Motion for transitions between screens
- **State:** Zustand or React Context depending on complexity

### Colour Token Setup
```js
// tailwind.config.js — extend with extracted palette
module.exports = {
  theme: {
    extend: {
      colors: {
        "brand-1": "#1a1a1a", // used 6751× in design
        "brand-2": "#ffffff", // used 1498× in design
        "brand-3": "#141414", // used 1324× in design
        "brand-4": "#999999", // used 375× in design
        "brand-5": "#703bf7", // used 180× in design
        "brand-6": "#333333", // used 106× in design
        "brand-7": "#666666", // used 75× in design
        "brand-8": "#262626", // used 33× in design
        "brand-9": "#000000", // used 23× in design
        "brand-10": "#0a0a0a", // used 19× in design
      }
    }
  }
}
```

### Font Setup
```css
/* Import detected font families */
@import url('https://fonts.googleapis.com/css2?family=Urbanist:wght@500;600;700&display=swap');
@import url('https://fonts.googleapis.com/css2?family=Inter:wght@400;500;600&display=swap');
```
